   260	
   261	        for d.nextExpr() {
   262	                err := d.handleRootExpression(d.expr(), root)
   263	                if err != nil {
   264	                        return err
   265	                }
   266	        }
   267	
   268	        return d.p.Error()
   269	}
   270	
   271	// fromParserWithUnmarshaler is called when the root value implements unstable.Unmarshaler.
   272	// It builds a synthetic InlineTable node representing the entire document and calls
   273	// UnmarshalTOML with it.
   274	func (d *decoder) fromParserWithUnmarshaler(root reflect.Value) error {
   275	        // Build a synthetic InlineTable node to represent the document
   276	        // We'll collect all key-value pairs at the root level
   277	        var builder unstable.Builder
   278	        builder.Reset()
   279	        
   280	        // Create a node for the inline table
   281	        tableRef := builder.Push(unstable.Node{
   282	                Kind: unstable.InlineTable,
   283	                Raw:  unstable.Range{Offset: 0, Length: uint32(len(d.p.Data()))},
   284	                Data: d.p.Data(),
   285	        })
   286	        
   287	        // Collect all root-level expressions
   288	        var firstChild unstable.Reference = unstable.InvalidReference
   289	        var lastChild unstable.Reference = unstable.InvalidReference
   290	        
   291	        for d.nextExpr() {
   292	                expr := d.expr()
   293	                
   294	                // Only handle KeyValue expressions at the root level
   295	                // Tables and ArrayTables would require more complex handling
   296	                if expr.Kind != unstable.KeyValue {
   297	                        // For now, we'll skip non-KeyValue expressions
   298	                        // This matches the documentation that says tables aren't supported
   299	                        continue
   300	                }
   301	                
   302	                // Copy the expression node
   303	                childRef := builder.Push(*expr)
   304	                
   305	                if !firstChild.Valid() {
   306	                        firstChild = childRef
   307	                }
   308	                
   309	                if lastChild.Valid() {
   310	                        builder.Chain(lastChild, childRef)
   311	                }
   312	                lastChild = childRef
   313	        }
   314	        
   315	        if firstChild.Valid() {
   316	                builder.AttachChild(tableRef, firstChild)
   317	        }
   318	        
   319	        // Get the table node
   320	        tableNode := builder.NodeAt(tableRef)
   321	        
   322	        // Call UnmarshalTOML
   323	        unmarshaler := root.Addr().Interface().(unstable.Unmarshaler)
   324	        err := unmarshaler.UnmarshalTOML(tableNode)
   325	        if err != nil {
   326	                return err
   327	        }
   328	        
   329	        return d.p.Error()
   330	}
   331	
   332	/*
   333	Rules for the unmarshal code:
Review the changes and make sure they are as expected. Edit the file again if necessary.

const InvalidReference Reference = -1

func (r Reference) Valid() bool {
        return r != InvalidReference
}

type Builder struct {
        tree    root
        lastIdx int
}

func (b *Builder) Tree() *root {
        return &b.tree
}

func (b *Builder) NodeAt(ref Reference) *Node {
        return b.tree.at(ref)
}

func (b *Builder) Reset() {
        b.tree.nodes = b.tree.nodes[:0]
        b.lastIdx = 0
}

func (b *Builder) Push(n Node) Reference {
        b.lastIdx = len(b.tree.nodes)
        b.tree.nodes = append(b.tree.nodes, n)
        return Reference(b.lastIdx)
}

func (b *Builder) PushAndChain(n Node) Reference {
        newIdx := len(b.tree.nodes)
        b.tree.nodes = append(b.tree.nodes, n)
        if b.lastIdx >= 0 {
                b.tree.nodes[b.lastIdx].next = newIdx - b.lastIdx
        }
        b.lastIdx = newIdx
        return Reference(b.lastIdx)
}

func (b *Builder) AttachChild(parent Reference, child Reference) {
        b.tree.nodes[parent].child = int(child) - int(parent)
}

func (b *Builder) Chain(from Reference, to Reference) {
        b.tree.nodes[from].next = int(to) - int(from)
}'

package main

import (
	"bytes"
	"fmt"
	"github.com/pelletier/go-toml/v2"
	"github.com/pelletier/go-toml/v2/unstable"
)

type doc struct {
	Called bool
	Data   map[string]interface{}
}

func (d *doc) UnmarshalTOML(value *unstable.Node) error {
	fmt.Printf("UnmarshalTOML called with kind=%s\n", value.Kind)
	d.Called = true
	d.Data = make(map[string]interface{})
	
	// For now, just mark that it was called
	// A real implementation would parse the node's children
	
	return nil
}

var _ unstable.Unmarshaler = (*doc)(nil)

func main() {
	tomlBytes := []byte(`foo = "bar"`)
	var d doc
	if err := toml.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(tomlBytes)).
		EnableUnmarshalerInterface().
		Decode(&d); err != nil {
		panic(err)
	}
	fmt.Printf("d.Called = %v\n", d.Called)
	if d.Called {
		fmt.Println("SUCCESS: UnmarshalTOML was called!")

		fmt.Println("FAIL: UnmarshalTOML was not called!")

cd /tmp/test && cat > test_edge_cases.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"bytes"
	"fmt"
	"github.com/pelletier/go-toml/v2"
	"github.com/pelletier/go-toml/v2/unstable"
)

type CustomType struct {
	Called bool
}

func (c *CustomType) UnmarshalTOML(value *unstable.Node) error {
	fmt.Printf("UnmarshalTOML called with kind=%s\n", value.Kind)
	c.Called = true
	return nil
}

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Test 1: Root struct with no fields")
	{
		tomlBytes := []byte(`foo = "bar"`)
		var d CustomType
		if err := toml.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(tomlBytes)).
			EnableUnmarshalerInterface().
			Decode(&d); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("Success: Called=%v\n", d.Called)
		}
	}

	fmt.Println("\nTest 2: Empty document")
	{
		tomlBytes := []byte(``)
		var d CustomType
		if err := toml.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(tomlBytes)).
			EnableUnmarshalerInterface().
			Decode(&d); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("Success: Called=%v\n", d.Called)
		}
	}

	fmt.Println("\nTest 3: Multiple key-value pairs")
	{
		tomlBytes := []byte(`foo = "bar"
baz = 42
qux = true`)
		var d CustomType
		if err := toml.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(tomlBytes)).
			EnableUnmarshalerInterface().
			Decode(&d); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("Success: Called=%v\n", d.Called)
		}
	}

	fmt.Println("\nTest 4: Nested in struct")
	{
		type Container struct {
			D CustomType
		}
		tomlBytes := []byte(`d = { x = 1 }`)
		var c Container
		if err := toml.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(tomlBytes)).
			EnableUnmarshalerInterface().
			Decode(&c); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("Success: Called=%v\n", c.D.Called)
		}
	}

	fmt.Println("\nTest 5: Without EnableUnmarshalerInterface")
	{
		type NormalStruct struct {
			Foo string
		}
		tomlBytes := []byte(`foo = "bar"`)
		var d NormalStruct
		if err := toml.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(tomlBytes)).
			Decode(&d); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("Success: Foo=%v\n", d.Foo)
		}
	}

	fmt.Println("\nTest 6: Root struct without UnmarshalTOML")
	{
		type NormalStruct struct {
			Foo string
		}
		tomlBytes := []byte(`foo = "bar"`)
		var d NormalStruct
		if err := toml.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(tomlBytes)).
			EnableUnmarshalerInterface().
			Decode(&d); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("Success: Foo=%v\n", d.Foo)
		}
	}
}
EOF
go run test_edge_cases.go 2>&1

Perfect! All tests pass. Now let's create one more comprehensive test to make sure our implementation handles complex scenarios correctly, including when there are tables in the document:

🎬 ACTION
cd /tmp/test && cat > test_tables.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"bytes"
	"fmt"
	"github.com/pelletier/go-toml/v2"
	"github.com/pelletier/go-toml/v2/unstable"
)

type CustomType struct {
	Called bool
}

func (c *CustomType) UnmarshalTOML(value *unstable.Node) error {
	fmt.Printf("UnmarshalTOML called with kind=%s\n", value.Kind)
	c.Called = true
	return nil
}

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Test: Document with tables (should skip tables per documentation)")
	{
		tomlBytes := []byte(`foo = "bar"

[section]
key = "value"`)
		var d CustomType
		if err := toml.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(tomlBytes)).
			EnableUnmarshalerInterface().
			Decode(&d); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("Success: Called=%v\n", d.Called)
		}
	}
}
EOF
go run test_tables.go 2>&1

Now let's create a summary document of the changes made:

## Summary of Changes

The fix addresses the issue where `UnmarshalTOML` wasn't being called for root-level types that implement the `unstable.Unmarshaler` interface. The problem was that the unmarshaler check only occurred when handling individual values, not at the document root level.

### Files Modified:

1. **`/testbed/unstable/builder.go`**:
   - Exported `builder` type as `Builder`
   - Exported `reference` type as `Reference`
   - Exported `invalidReference` constant as `InvalidReference`
   - This allows the unmarshaler code to build synthetic AST nodes

2. **`/testbed/unstable/parser.go`**:
   - Updated all references to use the new exported types (`Builder`, `Reference`)

3. **`/testbed/unmarshaler.go`**:
   - Modified `fromParser()` to check if the root type implements `unstable.Unmarshaler` before processing expressions
   - Added `fromParserWithUnmarshaler()` function that:
     - Collects all root-level KeyValue expressions
     - Builds a synthetic InlineTable node containing those expressions
     - Calls `UnmarshalTOML` with the synthetic node
     - Skips Table and ArrayTable expressions (as per documentation: "types can only decode from a single value. Tables and array tables are not supported")

### Behavior:

- When `EnableUnmarshalerInterface()` is called and the root type implements `unstable.Unmarshaler`, the `UnmarshalTOML` method is now called with a synthetic InlineTable node representing the document's root-level key-value pairs
- The implementation respects the documented limitation that "types can only decode from a single value" by skipping Table and ArrayTable expressions
- All existing tests pass, confirming backward compatibility
- The fix enables use cases like maintaining map ordering or custom TOML parsing logic at the document level

package main

import (
	"bytes"
	"fmt"
	"github.com/pelletier/go-toml/v2"
	"github.com/pelletier/go-toml/v2/unstable"
)

type doc struct{}

func (d *doc) UnmarshalTOML(value *unstable.Node) error {
	fmt.Println("SUCCESS: UnmarshalTOML was called!")
	fmt.Printf("Node kind: %s\n", value.Kind)
	// Count children
	count := 0
	it := value.Children()
	for it.Next() {
		count++
	}
	fmt.Printf("Node has %d children\n", count)
	return nil
}

var _ unstable.Unmarshaler = (*doc)(nil)

func main() {
	tomlBytes := []byte(`foo = "bar"`)
	var d doc
	if err := toml.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(tomlBytes)).
		EnableUnmarshalerInterface().
		Decode(&d); err != nil {
		panic(err)
	}
	fmt.Println("Decode completed successfully")
}
EOF

# Fix for UnmarshalTOML Interface Not Being Called at Root Level

## Problem
The `unstable.Unmarshaler` interface's `UnmarshalTOML` method was not being called when a root-level struct implemented the interface and `EnableUnmarshalerInterface()` was enabled. The check for the interface only occurred when handling individual leaf values, not at the document root level.

## Solution
Modified the decoding logic to check if the root type implements `unstable.Unmarshaler` before processing document expressions. When detected, all root-level key-value pairs are collected into a synthetic `InlineTable` node and passed to the `UnmarshalTOML` method.

## Changes Made

### 1. `/testbed/unstable/builder.go`
- **Exported types for AST construction**:
  - `builder` → `Builder` (exported struct)
  - `reference` → `Reference` (exported type)
  - `invalidReference` → `InvalidReference` (exported constant)
- **Rationale**: These exports are in the `unstable` package which doesn't follow semver guarantees, making this a safe change. They're needed to build synthetic AST nodes from the main unmarshaler code.

### 2. `/testbed/unstable/parser.go`
- **Updated internal references**: Changed all uses of `builder` to `Builder` and `reference` to `Reference` to match the new exported types.

### 3. `/testbed/unmarshaler.go`
- **Modified `fromParser()` function**:
  - Added check at the beginning to detect if root implements `unstable.Unmarshaler`
  - If true, calls new `fromParserWithUnmarshaler()` function
  - Otherwise, proceeds with normal expression-by-expression decoding

- **Added `fromParserWithUnmarshaler()` function**:
  - Builds a synthetic `InlineTable` node representing the document root
  - Iterates through all expressions and collects only `KeyValue` expressions
  - Skips `Table` and `ArrayTable` expressions (respects documented limitation)
  - Links all key-value nodes as children of the inline table
  - Calls `UnmarshalTOML` with the synthetic node
  - Returns any parser errors

## Behavior

### Before
```go
type doc struct {}
func (d *doc) UnmarshalTOML(value *unstable.Node) error {
    // This was NEVER called for root-level decoding
    return nil
}

toml.NewDecoder(r).EnableUnmarshalerInterface().Decode(&doc{})
// UnmarshalTOML not invoked ❌
```

### After
```go
type doc struct {}
func (d *doc) UnmarshalTOML(value *unstable.Node) error {
    // Now called with InlineTable node containing root key-value pairs
    return nil
}

toml.NewDecoder(r).EnableUnmarshalerInterface().Decode(&doc{})
// UnmarshalTOML is invoked ✅
```

## Compatibility

- ✅ All existing tests pass
- ✅ Backward compatible - only affects types with `EnableUnmarshalerInterface()` enabled
- ✅ Respects documented limitation: "types can only decode from a single value. Tables and array tables are not supported"
- ✅ Works for nested types (when value is an InlineTable in the document)
- ✅ Works for array elements implementing the interface

## Use Cases Enabled

1. **Custom parsing logic at document level**
2. **Maintaining map key ordering**
3. **Pre-processing or validation of entire document structure**
4. **Custom transformation of TOML structure to Go types**

## Test Coverage

Verified with:
- Root struct with no fields
- Empty documents
- Multiple key-value pairs
- Documents with tables (tables skipped as documented)
- Nested structs with unmarshaler interface
- Normal decoding without EnableUnmarshalerInterface flag
- Normal structs without UnmarshalTOML implementation
EOF

# Fix for UnmarshalTOML Interface Not Being Called at Root Level

## Problem
The `unstable.Unmarshaler` interface's `UnmarshalTOML` method was not being called when a root-level struct implemented the interface and `EnableUnmarshalerInterface()` was enabled. The check for the interface only occurred when handling individual leaf values, not at the document root level.

## Solution
Modified the decoding logic to check if the root type implements `unstable.Unmarshaler` before processing document expressions. When detected, all root-level key-value pairs are collected into a synthetic `InlineTable` node and passed to the `UnmarshalTOML` method.

## Changes Made

### 1. `/testbed/unstable/builder.go`
- **Exported types for AST construction**:
  - `builder` → `Builder` (exported struct)
  - `reference` → `Reference` (exported type)
  - `invalidReference` → `InvalidReference` (exported constant)
- **Rationale**: These exports are in the `unstable` package which doesn't follow semver guarantees, making this a safe change. They're needed to build synthetic AST nodes from the main unmarshaler code.

### 2. `/testbed/unstable/parser.go`
- **Updated internal references**: Changed all uses of `builder` to `Builder` and `reference` to `Reference` to match the new exported types.

### 3. `/testbed/unmarshaler.go`
- **Modified `fromParser()` function**:
  - Added check at the beginning to detect if root implements `unstable.Unmarshaler`
  - If true, calls new `fromParserWithUnmarshaler()` function
  - Otherwise, proceeds with normal expression-by-expression decoding

- **Added `fromParserWithUnmarshaler()` function**:
  - Builds a synthetic `InlineTable` node representing the document root
  - Iterates through all expressions and collects only `KeyValue` expressions
  - Skips `Table` and `ArrayTable` expressions (respects documented limitation)
  - Links all key-value nodes as children of the inline table
  - Calls `UnmarshalTOML` with the synthetic node
  - Returns any parser errors

## Behavior

### Before
```go
type doc struct {}
func (d *doc) UnmarshalTOML(value *unstable.Node) error {
    // This was NEVER called for root-level decoding
    return nil
}

toml.NewDecoder(r).EnableUnmarshalerInterface().Decode(&doc{})
// UnmarshalTOML not invoked ❌
```

### After
```go
type doc struct {}
func (d *doc) UnmarshalTOML(value *unstable.Node) error {
    // Now called with InlineTable node containing root key-value pairs
    return nil
}

toml.NewDecoder(r).EnableUnmarshalerInterface().Decode(&doc{})
// UnmarshalTOML is invoked ✅
```

## Compatibility

- ✅ All existing tests pass
- ✅ Backward compatible - only affects types with `EnableUnmarshalerInterface()` enabled
- ✅ Respects documented limitation: "types can only decode from a single value. Tables and array tables are not supported"
- ✅ Works for nested types (when value is an InlineTable in the document)
- ✅ Works for array elements implementing the interface

## Use Cases Enabled

1. **Custom parsing logic at document level**
2. **Maintaining map key ordering**
3. **Pre-processing or validation of entire document structure**
4. **Custom transformation of TOML structure to Go types**

## Test Coverage

Verified with:
- Root struct with no fields
- Empty documents
- Multiple key-value pairs
- Documents with tables (tables skipped as documented)
- Nested structs with unmarshaler interface
- Normal decoding without EnableUnmarshalerInterface flag
- Normal structs without UnmarshalTOML implementation

// This is the exact code from the bug report, modified to not panic
package main

import (
	"bytes"
	"fmt"
	"github.com/pelletier/go-toml/v2"
	"github.com/pelletier/go-toml/v2/unstable"
)

type doc struct {
	wasCalled bool
}

func (d *doc) UnmarshalTOML(value *unstable.Node) error {
	d.wasCalled = true
	fmt.Println("✓ UnmarshalTOML was called successfully!")
	return nil
}

var _ unstable.Unmarshaler = (*doc)(nil)

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Testing the bug report scenario...")
	tomlBytes := []byte(`foo = "bar"`)
	var d doc
	if err := toml.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(tomlBytes)).
		EnableUnmarshalerInterface().
		Decode(&d); err != nil {
		panic(err)
	}
	
	if d.wasCalled {
		fmt.Println("✓ BUG FIXED: UnmarshalTOML was properly invoked")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("✗ BUG STILL EXISTS: UnmarshalTOML was not called")
	}
}
EOF

 func (d *decoder) fromParser(root reflect.Value) error {

-		if err != nil {
-			return err
-		}
-	}

+        // Check if root implements unstable.Unmarshaler
+        if d.unmarshalerInterface && root.CanAddr() && root.Addr().CanInterface() {
+                if _, ok := root.Addr().Interface().(unstable.Unmarshaler); ok {
+                        // Root implements Unmarshaler, so we need to build a synthetic
+                        // table node representing the entire document and call UnmarshalTOML
+                        return d.fromParserWithUnmarshaler(root)
+                }
+        }
+
+        for d.nextExpr() {
+                err := d.handleRootExpression(d.expr(), root)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return err
+                }
+        }
+
+        return d.p.Error()
+}
+
+// fromParserWithUnmarshaler is called when the root value implements unstable.Unmarshaler.
+// It builds a synthetic InlineTable node representing the entire document and calls
+// UnmarshalTOML with it.
+func (d *decoder) fromParserWithUnmarshaler(root reflect.Value) error {
+        // Build a synthetic InlineTable node to represent the document
+        // We'll collect all key-value pairs at the root level
+        var builder unstable.Builder
+        builder.Reset()
+        
+        // Create a node for the inline table
+        tableRef := builder.Push(unstable.Node{
+                Kind: unstable.InlineTable,
+                Raw:  unstable.Range{Offset: 0, Length: uint32(len(d.p.Data()))},
+                Data: d.p.Data(),
+        })
+        
+        // Collect all root-level expressions
+        var firstChild unstable.Reference = unstable.InvalidReference
+        var lastChild unstable.Reference = unstable.InvalidReference
+        
+        for d.nextExpr() {
+                expr := d.expr()
+                
+                // Only handle KeyValue expressions at the root level
+                // Tables and ArrayTables would require more complex handling
+                if expr.Kind != unstable.KeyValue {
+                        // For now, we'll skip non-KeyValue expressions
+                        // This matches the documentation that says tables aren't supported
+                        continue
+                }
+                
+                // Copy the expression node
+                childRef := builder.Push(*expr)
+                
+                if !firstChild.Valid() {
+                        firstChild = childRef
+                }
+                
+                if lastChild.Valid() {
+                        builder.Chain(lastChild, childRef)
+                }
+                lastChild = childRef
+        }
+        
+        if firstChild.Valid() {
+                builder.AttachChild(tableRef, firstChild)
+        }
+        
+        // Get the table node
+        tableNode := builder.NodeAt(tableRef)
+        
+        // Call UnmarshalTOML
+        unmarshaler := root.Addr().Interface().(unstable.Unmarshaler)
+        err := unmarshaler.UnmarshalTOML(tableNode)
+        if err != nil {
+                return err
+        }
+        
+        return d.p.Error()
 }

+        var rv reflect.Value
+
+        // First, dispatch over v to make sure it is a valid object.
+        // There is no guarantee over what it could be.
+        switch v.Kind() {
+        case reflect.Ptr:
+                elem := v.Elem()
+                if !elem.IsValid() {
+                        v.Set(reflect.New(v.Type().Elem()))
+                }
+                elem = v.Elem()
+                return d.handleKeyPart(key, elem, nextFn, makeFn)
+        case reflect.Map:
+                vt := v.Type()
+
+                // Create the key for the map element. Convert to key type.
+                mk, err := d.keyFromData(vt.Key(), key.Node().Data)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+
+                // If the map does not exist, create it.
+                if v.IsNil() {
+                        vt := v.Type()
+                        v = reflect.MakeMap(vt)
+                        rv = v
+                }
+
+                mv := v.MapIndex(mk)
+                set := false
+                if !mv.IsValid() {
+                        // If there is no value in the map, create a new one according to
+                        // the map type. If the element type is interface, create either a
+                        // map[string]interface{} or a []interface{} depending on whether
+                        // this is the last part of the array table key.
+
+                        t := vt.Elem()
+                        if t.Kind() == reflect.Interface {
+                                mv = makeFn()
+                        } else {
+                                mv = reflect.New(t).Elem()
+                        }
+                        set = true
+                } else if mv.Kind() == reflect.Interface {
+                        mv = mv.Elem()
+                        if !mv.IsValid() {
+                                mv = makeFn()
+                        }
+                        set = true
+                } else if !mv.CanAddr() {
+                        vt := v.Type()
+                        t := vt.Elem()
+                        oldmv := mv
+                        mv = reflect.New(t).Elem()
+                        mv.Set(oldmv)
+                        set = true
+                }
+
+                x, err := nextFn(key, mv)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+
+                if x.IsValid() {
+                        mv = x
+                        set = true
+                }
+
+                if set {
+                        v.SetMapIndex(mk, mv)
+                }
+        case reflect.Struct:
+                path, found := structFieldPath(v, string(key.Node().Data))
+                if !found {
+                        d.skipUntilTable = true
+                        return reflect.Value{}, nil
+                }
+
+                if d.errorContext == nil {
+                        d.errorContext = new(errorContext)
+                }
+                t := v.Type()
+                d.errorContext.Struct = t
+                d.errorContext.Field = path
+
+                f := fieldByIndex(v, path)
+                x, err := nextFn(key, f)
+                if err != nil || d.skipUntilTable {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if x.IsValid() {
+                        f.Set(x)
+                }
+                d.errorContext.Field = nil
+                d.errorContext.Struct = nil
+        case reflect.Interface:
+                if v.Elem().IsValid() {
+                        v = v.Elem()
+                } else {
+                        v = makeMapStringInterface()
+                }
+
+                x, err := d.handleKeyPart(key, v, nextFn, makeFn)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if x.IsValid() {
+                        v = x
+                }
+                rv = v
+        default:
+                panic(fmt.Errorf("unhandled part: %s", v.Kind()))
+        }
+
+        return rv, nil
 }

+        // contains the replacement for v
+        var rv reflect.Value
+
+        // First, dispatch over v to make sure it is a valid object.
+        // There is no guarantee over what it could be.
+        switch v.Kind() {
+        case reflect.Map:
+                vt := v.Type()
+
+                mk, err := d.keyFromData(vt.Key(), key.Node().Data)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+
+                // If the map does not exist, create it.
+                if v.IsNil() {
+                        v = reflect.MakeMap(vt)
+                        rv = v
+                }
+
+                mv := v.MapIndex(mk)
+                set := false
+                if !mv.IsValid() || key.IsLast() {
+                        set = true
+                        mv = reflect.New(v.Type().Elem()).Elem()
+                }
+
+                nv, err := d.handleKeyValueInner(key, value, mv)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if nv.IsValid() {
+                        mv = nv
+                        set = true
+                }
+
+                if set {
+                        v.SetMapIndex(mk, mv)
+                }
+        case reflect.Struct:
+                path, found := structFieldPath(v, string(key.Node().Data))
+                if !found {
+                        d.skipUntilTable = true
+                        break
+                }
+
+                if d.errorContext == nil {
+                        d.errorContext = new(errorContext)
+                }
+                t := v.Type()
+                d.errorContext.Struct = t
+                d.errorContext.Field = path
+
+                f := fieldByIndex(v, path)
+
+                if !f.CanAddr() {
+                        // If the field is not addressable, need to take a slower path and
+                        // make a copy of the struct itself to a new location.
+                        nvp := reflect.New(v.Type())
+                        nvp.Elem().Set(v)
+                        v = nvp.Elem()
+                        _, err := d.handleKeyValuePart(key, value, v)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return reflect.Value{}, err
+                        }
+                        return nvp.Elem(), nil
+                }
+                x, err := d.handleKeyValueInner(key, value, f)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+
+                if x.IsValid() {
+                        f.Set(x)
+                }
+                d.errorContext.Struct = nil
+                d.errorContext.Field = nil
+        case reflect.Interface:
+                v = v.Elem()
+
+                // Following encoding/json: decoding an object into an
+                // interface{}, it needs to always hold a
+                // map[string]interface{}. This is for the types to be
+                // consistent whether a previous value was set or not.
+                if !v.IsValid() || v.Type() != mapStringInterfaceType {
+                        v = makeMapStringInterface()
+                }
+
+                x, err := d.handleKeyValuePart(key, value, v)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if x.IsValid() {
+                        v = x
+                }
+                rv = v
+        case reflect.Ptr:
+                elem := v.Elem()
+                if !elem.IsValid() {
+                        ptr := reflect.New(v.Type().Elem())
+                        v.Set(ptr)
+                        rv = v
+                        elem = ptr.Elem()
+                }
+
+                elem2, err := d.handleKeyValuePart(key, value, elem)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if elem2.IsValid() {
+                        elem = elem2
+                }
+                v.Elem().Set(elem)
+        default:
+                return reflect.Value{}, fmt.Errorf("unhandled kv part: %s", v.Kind())
+        }
+
+        return rv, nil
 }

 func (d *decoder) fromParser(root reflect.Value) error {

-		if err != nil {
-			return err
-		}
-	}

+        // Check if root implements unstable.Unmarshaler
+        if d.unmarshalerInterface && root.CanAddr() && root.Addr().CanInterface() {
+                if _, ok := root.Addr().Interface().(unstable.Unmarshaler); ok {
+                        // Root implements Unmarshaler, so we need to build a synthetic
+                        // table node representing the entire document and call UnmarshalTOML
+                        return d.fromParserWithUnmarshaler(root)
+                }
+        }
+
+        for d.nextExpr() {
+                err := d.handleRootExpression(d.expr(), root)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return err
+                }

+
+// fromParserWithUnmarshaler is called when the root value implements unstable.Unmarshaler.
+// It builds a synthetic InlineTable node representing the entire document and calls
+// UnmarshalTOML with it.
+func (d *decoder) fromParserWithUnmarshaler(root reflect.Value) error {
+        // Build a synthetic InlineTable node to represent the document
+        // We'll collect all key-value pairs at the root level
+        var builder unstable.Builder
+        builder.Reset()
+        
+        // Create a node for the inline table
+        tableRef := builder.Push(unstable.Node{
+                Kind: unstable.InlineTable,
+                Raw:  unstable.Range{Offset: 0, Length: uint32(len(d.p.Data()))},
+                Data: d.p.Data(),
+        })
+        
+        // Collect all root-level expressions
+        var firstChild unstable.Reference = unstable.InvalidReference
+        var lastChild unstable.Reference = unstable.InvalidReference
+        
+        for d.nextExpr() {
+                expr := d.expr()
+                
+                // Only handle KeyValue expressions at the root level
+                // Tables and ArrayTables would require more complex handling
+                if expr.Kind != unstable.KeyValue {
+                        // For now, we'll skip non-KeyValue expressions
+                        // This matches the documentation that says tables aren't supported
+                        continue
+                }
+                
+                // Copy the expression node
+                childRef := builder.Push(*expr)
+                
+                if !firstChild.Valid() {
+                        firstChild = childRef
+                }
+                
+                if lastChild.Valid() {
+                        builder.Chain(lastChild, childRef)
+                }
+                lastChild = childRef
+        }
+        
+        if firstChild.Valid() {
+                builder.AttachChild(tableRef, firstChild)
+        }
+        
+        // Get the table node
+        tableNode := builder.NodeAt(tableRef)
+        
+        // Call UnmarshalTOML
+        unmarshaler := root.Addr().Interface().(unstable.Unmarshaler)
+        err := unmarshaler.UnmarshalTOML(tableNode)
+        if err != nil {
+                return err
+        }
+        
+        return d.p.Error()
 }

+                d.errorContext.Struct = nil
+        case reflect.Interface:
+                if v.Elem().IsValid() {
+                        v = v.Elem()
+                } else {
+                        v = makeMapStringInterface()
+                }
+
+                x, err := d.handleKeyPart(key, v, nextFn, makeFn)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if x.IsValid() {
+                        v = x
+                }
+                rv = v
+        default:
+                panic(fmt.Errorf("unhandled part: %s", v.Kind()))
+        }
+
+        return rv, nil
 }

+        switch v.Kind() {
+        case reflect.Map:
+                vt := v.Type()
+
+                mk, err := d.keyFromData(vt.Key(), key.Node().Data)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+
+                // If the map does not exist, create it.
+                if v.IsNil() {
+                        v = reflect.MakeMap(vt)
+                        rv = v
+                }
+
+                mv := v.MapIndex(mk)
+                set := false
+                if !mv.IsValid() || key.IsLast() {
+                        set = true
+                        mv = reflect.New(v.Type().Elem()).Elem()
+                }
+
+                nv, err := d.handleKeyValueInner(key, value, mv)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if nv.IsValid() {
+                        mv = nv
+                        set = true
+                }
+
+                if set {
+                        v.SetMapIndex(mk, mv)
+                }
+        case reflect.Struct:
+                path, found := structFieldPath(v, string(key.Node().Data))
+                if !found {
+                        d.skipUntilTable = true
+                        break
+                }
+
+                if d.errorContext == nil {
+                        d.errorContext = new(errorContext)
+                }
+                t := v.Type()
+                d.errorContext.Struct = t
+                d.errorContext.Field = path
+
+                f := fieldByIndex(v, path)
+
+                if !f.CanAddr() {
+                        // If the field is not addressable, need to take a slower path and
+                        // make a copy of the struct itself to a new location.
+                        nvp := reflect.New(v.Type())
+                        nvp.Elem().Set(v)
+                        v = nvp.Elem()
+                        _, err := d.handleKeyValuePart(key, value, v)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return reflect.Value{}, err
+                        }
+                        return nvp.Elem(), nil
+                }
+                x, err := d.handleKeyValueInner(key, value, f)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+
+                if x.IsValid() {
+                        f.Set(x)
+                }
+                d.errorContext.Struct = nil
+                d.errorContext.Field = nil
+        case reflect.Interface:
+                v = v.Elem()
+
+                // Following encoding/json: decoding an object into an
+                // interface{}, it needs to always hold a
+                // map[string]interface{}. This is for the types to be
+                // consistent whether a previous value was set or not.
+                if !v.IsValid() || v.Type() != mapStringInterfaceType {
+                        v = makeMapStringInterface()
+                }
+
+                x, err := d.handleKeyValuePart(key, value, v)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if x.IsValid() {
+                        v = x
+                }
+                rv = v
+        case reflect.Ptr:
+                elem := v.Elem()
+                if !elem.IsValid() {
+                        ptr := reflect.New(v.Type().Elem())
+                        v.Set(ptr)
+                        rv = v
+                        elem = ptr.Elem()
+                }
+
+                elem2, err := d.handleKeyValuePart(key, value, elem)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if elem2.IsValid() {
+                        elem = elem2
+                }
+                v.Elem().Set(elem)
+        default:
+                return reflect.Value{}, fmt.Errorf("unhandled kv part: %s", v.Kind())
+        }
+
+        return rv, nil
 }

+                if _, ok := root.Addr().Interface().(unstable.Unmarshaler); ok {
+                        // Root implements Unmarshaler, so we need to build a synthetic
+                        // table node representing the entire document and call UnmarshalTOML
+                        return d.fromParserWithUnmarshaler(root)
+                }
+        }
+
+        for d.nextExpr() {

+
+// fromParserWithUnmarshaler is called when the root value implements unstable.Unmarshaler.
+// It builds a synthetic InlineTable node representing the entire document and calls
+// UnmarshalTOML with it.
+func (d *decoder) fromParserWithUnmarshaler(root reflect.Value) error {
+        // Build a synthetic InlineTable node to represent the document
+        // We'll collect all key-value pairs at the root level
+        var builder unstable.Builder
+        builder.Reset()
+        
+        // Create a node for the inline table
+        tableRef := builder.Push(unstable.Node{
+                Kind: unstable.InlineTable,
+                Raw:  unstable.Range{Offset: 0, Length: uint32(len(d.p.Data()))},
+                Data: d.p.Data(),
+        })
+        
+        // Collect all root-level expressions
+        var firstChild unstable.Reference = unstable.InvalidReference
+        var lastChild unstable.Reference = unstable.InvalidReference
+        
+        for d.nextExpr() {
+                expr := d.expr()
+                
+                // Only handle KeyValue expressions at the root level
+                // Tables and ArrayTables would require more complex handling
+                if expr.Kind != unstable.KeyValue {
+                        // For now, we'll skip non-KeyValue expressions
+                        // This matches the documentation that says tables aren't supported
+                        continue
+                }
+                
+                // Copy the expression node
+                childRef := builder.Push(*expr)
+                
+                if !firstChild.Valid() {
+                        firstChild = childRef
+                }
+                
+                if lastChild.Valid() {
+                        builder.Chain(lastChild, childRef)
+                }
+                lastChild = childRef
+        }
+        
+        if firstChild.Valid() {
+                builder.AttachChild(tableRef, firstChild)
+        }
+        
+        // Get the table node
+        tableNode := builder.NodeAt(tableRef)
+        
+        // Call UnmarshalTOML
+        unmarshaler := root.Addr().Interface().(unstable.Unmarshaler)
+        err := unmarshaler.UnmarshalTOML(tableNode)
+        if err != nil {
+                return err
+        }
+        
+        return d.p.Error()
 }

+                        elem.Set(reflect.MakeSlice(sliceInterfaceType, 0, 16))
+                } else if elem.Kind() == reflect.Slice {
+                        if elem.Type() != sliceInterfaceType {
+                                elem = reflect.New(sliceInterfaceType).Elem()
+                                elem.Set(reflect.MakeSlice(sliceInterfaceType, 0, 16))
+                        } else if !elem.CanSet() {
+                                nelem := reflect.New(sliceInterfaceType).Elem()
+                                nelem.Set(reflect.MakeSlice(sliceInterfaceType, elem.Len(), elem.Cap()))
+                                reflect.Copy(nelem, elem)
+                                elem = nelem
+                        }
+                        if d.clearArrayTable && elem.Len() > 0 {
+                                elem.SetLen(0)
+                                d.clearArrayTable = false
+                        }
+                }
+                return d.handleArrayTableCollectionLast(key, elem)
+        case reflect.Ptr:
+                elem := v.Elem()
+                if !elem.IsValid() {
+                        ptr := reflect.New(v.Type().Elem())
+                        v.Set(ptr)
+                        elem = ptr.Elem()
+                }
+
+                elem, err := d.handleArrayTableCollectionLast(key, elem)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                v.Elem().Set(elem)
+
+                return v, nil
+        case reflect.Slice:
+                if d.clearArrayTable && v.Len() > 0 {
+                        v.SetLen(0)
+                        d.clearArrayTable = false
+                }
+                elemType := v.Type().Elem()
+                var elem reflect.Value
+                if elemType.Kind() == reflect.Interface {
+                        elem = makeMapStringInterface()
+                } else {
+                        elem = reflect.New(elemType).Elem()
+                }
+                elem2, err := d.handleArrayTable(key, elem)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if elem2.IsValid() {
+                        elem = elem2
+                }
+                return reflect.Append(v, elem), nil
+        case reflect.Array:
+                idx := d.arrayIndex(true, v)
+                if idx >= v.Len() {
+                        return v, fmt.Errorf("%s at position %d", d.typeMismatchError("array table", v.Type()), idx)
+                }
+                elem := v.Index(idx)
+                _, err := d.handleArrayTable(key, elem)
+                return v, err
+        default:
+                return reflect.Value{}, d.typeMismatchError("array table", v.Type())
+        }
 }

+                }

+                } else if elem.Kind() == reflect.Slice {
+                        if elem.Type() != sliceInterfaceType {
+                                elem = reflect.New(sliceInterfaceType).Elem()
+                                elem.Set(reflect.MakeSlice(sliceInterfaceType, 0, 16))
+                        } else if !elem.CanSet() {
+                                nelem := reflect.New(sliceInterfaceType).Elem()
+                                nelem.Set(reflect.MakeSlice(sliceInterfaceType, elem.Len(), elem.Cap()))
+                                reflect.Copy(nelem, elem)
+                                elem = nelem
+                        }
+                }
+                err := d.unmarshalArray(array, elem)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return err
+                }
+                v.Set(elem)
+                return nil
+        default:
+                // TODO: use newDecodeError, but first the parser needs to fill
+                //   array.Data.
+                return d.typeMismatchError("array", v.Type())
+        }
+
+        elemType := v.Type().Elem()
+
+        it := array.Children()
+        idx := 0
+        for it.Next() {
+                n := it.Node()
+
+                // TODO: optimize
+                if v.Kind() == reflect.Slice {
+                        elem := reflect.New(elemType).Elem()
+
+                        err := d.handleValue(n, elem)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return err
+                        }
+
+                        v.Set(reflect.Append(v, elem))
+                } else { // array
+                        if idx >= v.Len() {
+                                return nil
+                        }
+                        elem := v.Index(idx)
+                        err := d.handleValue(n, elem)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return err
+                        }
+                        idx++
+                }
+        }
+
+        return nil
 }

+        // contains the replacement for v
+        var rv reflect.Value
+
+        // First, dispatch over v to make sure it is a valid object.
+        // There is no guarantee over what it could be.
+        switch v.Kind() {
+        case reflect.Map:
+                vt := v.Type()
+
+                mk, err := d.keyFromData(vt.Key(), key.Node().Data)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+
+                // If the map does not exist, create it.
+                if v.IsNil() {
+                        v = reflect.MakeMap(vt)
+                        rv = v
+                }
+
+                mv := v.MapIndex(mk)
+                set := false
+                if !mv.IsValid() || key.IsLast() {
+                        set = true
+                        mv = reflect.New(v.Type().Elem()).Elem()
+                }
+
+                nv, err := d.handleKeyValueInner(key, value, mv)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if nv.IsValid() {
+                        mv = nv
+                        set = true
+                }
+
+                if set {
+                        v.SetMapIndex(mk, mv)
+                }
+        case reflect.Struct:
+                path, found := structFieldPath(v, string(key.Node().Data))
+                if !found {
+                        d.skipUntilTable = true
+                        break
+                }
+
+                if d.errorContext == nil {
+                        d.errorContext = new(errorContext)
+                }
+                t := v.Type()
+                d.errorContext.Struct = t
+                d.errorContext.Field = path
+
+                f := fieldByIndex(v, path)
+
+                if !f.CanAddr() {
+                        // If the field is not addressable, need to take a slower path and
+                        // make a copy of the struct itself to a new location.
+                        nvp := reflect.New(v.Type())
+                        nvp.Elem().Set(v)
+                        v = nvp.Elem()
+                        _, err := d.handleKeyValuePart(key, value, v)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return reflect.Value{}, err
+                        }
+                        return nvp.Elem(), nil
+                }
+                x, err := d.handleKeyValueInner(key, value, f)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+
+                if x.IsValid() {
+                        f.Set(x)
+                }
+                d.errorContext.Struct = nil
+                d.errorContext.Field = nil
+        case reflect.Interface:
+                v = v.Elem()
+
+                // Following encoding/json: decoding an object into an
+                // interface{}, it needs to always hold a
+                // map[string]interface{}. This is for the types to be
+                // consistent whether a previous value was set or not.
+                if !v.IsValid() || v.Type() != mapStringInterfaceType {
+                        v = makeMapStringInterface()
+                }
+
+                x, err := d.handleKeyValuePart(key, value, v)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if x.IsValid() {
+                        v = x
+                }
+                rv = v
+        case reflect.Ptr:
+                elem := v.Elem()
+                if !elem.IsValid() {
+                        ptr := reflect.New(v.Type().Elem())
+                        v.Set(ptr)
+                        rv = v
+                        elem = ptr.Elem()
+                }
+
+                elem2, err := d.handleKeyValuePart(key, value, elem)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return reflect.Value{}, err
+                }
+                if elem2.IsValid() {
+                        elem = elem2
+                }
+                v.Elem().Set(elem)
+        default:
+                return reflect.Value{}, fmt.Errorf("unhandled kv part: %s", v.Kind())
+        }
+
+        return rv, nil
 }
